1	import logging
2	
3	import click
4	
5	from tim.cliagent import CliAgent
6	from tim import MacSandboxProject
7	
8	
9	def _configure_logging(verbosity: int) -> None:
10	    if verbosity == 0:
11	        return
12	    log_level = logging.INFO
13	    if verbosity > 1:
14	        log_level = logging.DEBUG
15	    stream_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
16	    stream_handler.addFilter(lambda record: record.name.startswith("tim."))
17	    stream_handler.setLevel(log_level)
18	    logging.basicConfig(level=log_level, handlers=[stream_handler])
19	
20	
21	@click.group(invoke_without_command=True)
22	@click.option("-v", "--verbose", count=True, default=0)
23	def main(verbose: int) -> None:
24	    _configure_logging(verbose)
25	    ctx = click.get_current_context()
26	
27	    if ctx.invoked_subcommand is None:
28	        project = MacSandboxProject.cwd()
29	        agent = CliAgent(project)

Key observations from the log format:
- `source.agent` - the agent name
- `source.agent_instance` - the agent instance ID
- `at` - timestamp
- `message.role` - "system", "user", "assistant", or "tool"
- `message.content` - the message content (may be empty for assistant)
- `message.reasoning` - reasoning text for assistant messages
- `message.tool_calls` - list of tool calls for assistant messages
- `message.id` - tool call ID (for tool messages)
- `message.name` - tool name (for tool messages)
- `usage` - token usage info

For the HTML:
- Each log entry becomes a block
- System messages in a distinct style
- User messages in a user style
- Assistant messages with collapsible reasoning and tool calls
- Tool messages (outputs) in a collapsible section

24	def parse_log_file(log_path: Path) -> list[LogMessage]:
25	    messages: list[LogMessage] = []
26	    with open(log_path, encoding="utf-8") as log_file:

28	            line_stripped = line.strip()
29	            if not line_stripped:

31	            record = json.loads(line_stripped)

64	def _format_tool_arguments(arguments_str: str) -> str:
65	    try:
66	        parsed = json.loads(arguments_str)
67	        return json.dumps(parsed, indent=2)
68	    except (json.JSONDecodeError, TypeError):
69	        return arguments_str

72	def _render_tool_call(tool_call: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
73	    tool_id = tool_call.get("id", "")

85	    content_escaped = escape(content)

87	    if len(content_escaped) > 120:
88	        preview += "..."
89	    return (
90	        f'<details class="tool-output">'

98	    if not tool_id:
99	        return "unknown"
100	    return tool_id

103	def _render_system(content: str) -> str:
104	    escaped_content = escape(content)
105	    preview = escaped_content[:100]
106	    if len(escaped_content) > 100:
107	        preview += "..."
108	    return (

128	def _render_assistant(content: str, reasoning: str | None, tool_calls: list[dict[str, Any]] | None) -> str:
129	    parts: list[str] = []
130	    if reasoning:
131	        parts.append(_render_reasoning(reasoning))
132	    if content:
133	        parts.append(f"<div class='message-content'><pre>{escape(content)}</pre></div>")
134	    if tool_calls:
135	        for tool_call in tool_calls:
136	            parts.append(_render_tool_call(tool_call))
137	    return f"<div class='message assistant'>{''.join(parts)}</div>"

140	def _render_reasoning(reasoning: str) -> str:

146	        f"</details>"

150	def render_html(messages: list[LogMessage], log_path: Path) -> str:
151	    agent_name = messages[0].agent if messages else "Unknown"
152	    sections = [_header_section(messages, agent_name, log_path)]
153	    for message in messages:
154	        sections.append(_message_section(message))
155	    return (

173	def _header_section(messages: list[LogMessage], agent_name: str, log_path: Path) -> str:
174	    entry_count = len(messages)
175	    timestamp = messages[0].timestamp if messages else ""
176	    return (
177	        f'<div class="header">'

185	    label = _agent_label(message.agent, message.agent_instance)

194	        f"</div>"

198	def _format_timestamp_display(timestamp: str) -> str:
199	    if not timestamp:
200	        return ""
201	    try:
202	        from datetime import datetime
203

205	        return dt.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")

210	def _render_message_body(message: LogMessage) -> str:
211	    if message.role == "system":

```python
def parse_log_file(log_path: Path) -> list[LogMessage]:
    messages: list[LogMessage] = []
    with open(log_path, encoding="utf-8") as log_file:
        for line in log_file:
            line_stripped = line.strip()
            if not line_stripped:
                continue
            record = _parse_record(line_stripped)
            messages.append(_build_log_message(record))
    return messages
```
